###########################
### Homefront Mechanic  ###

USA_proxy_war_homefront_GUI = {
	USA_SAW_increase_manpower_timer = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		days_mission_timeout = 70
		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 1

		priority = 100

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = yes }
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = no
				has_country_flag = USA_homefront_mech_active
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_SAW_increase_manpower_timer"
			USA_service_manpower_pulse_positive = yes
		}
	}
	USA_SAW_decrease_manpower_timer = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat_alternate
		days_mission_timeout = 70
		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 1

		priority = 100

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = no }
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = yes
				has_country_flag = USA_homefront_mech_active
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_SAW_decrease_manpower_timer"
			USA_service_manpower_pulse_negative = yes
		}
	}

	USA_WAC_discontent_declines = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat_alternate
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 7
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent = 0 }
				tooltip = USA_WAC_discontent_is_gone_tt
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision complete USA_WAC_discontent_declines"
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_WAC_discontent_declines"
			USA_WAC_discontent_decrease = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 0 } }
					activate_mission = USA_WAC_discontent_declines
				}
				else = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_WAC_discontent }
					clear_variable = WAC_discontent_stability
					clear_variable = WAC_discontent_war_support
					clear_variable = WAC_discontent_political_power
				}
			}

		}
	}

	USA_SAW_reduce_hawkishness = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		days_mission_timeout = 70
		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 1

		priority = 100

		cancel_trigger = {
			USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = yes
		}

		activation = {
			USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = no
			check_variable = { USA_hawkishness > 0 }
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_SAW_reduce_hawkishness"
			USA_decrease_hawkishness_small = yes
		}
	}

	USA_Homefront_buy_commpower = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_supply

		days_re_enable = 15

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}

		cost = 50

		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = no

		remove_effect = {
			add_command_power = 25
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_intensify_OFN_propaganda = {

		}

		ai_will_do = {

			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_low = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_low = yes
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
			#WIN = { check_variable = { WIN_foreign_intervention > 40 } }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { GDP > 0 } }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_50_million

		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders_cost
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { removed_from_reserves = money_reserves }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = removed_from_reserves min = 0 max = 0.05 }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = removed_from_reserves }
				add_to_variable = { national_debt = to_add_to_debt }
			}
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_blackmail_independence_activists = {
		icon = GFX_decision_document_cancel
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
			#WIN = { check_variable = { WIN_foreign_intervention > 75 } }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_us_intervention > 75 }
			}
		}

		cost = 35

		days_remove = 21
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_high = yes
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_foreign_intervention_medium_us = yes

			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum_trigger
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed < 3 }
			}
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}
		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = no

		cost = 15

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed > 0 }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum_effect

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 0 } }
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening }
				} else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 1 } }
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening_2 }
				} else = {
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening_3 }
			}


			hidden_effect = {
				WIN = {
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_days_left = 7 }
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_days_max = 7 }
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 1 }


					# Recompute clock
					set_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = 100 }
					multiply_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = WIN_referendum_days_left }
					divide_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = WIN_referendum_days_max }
				}

			}
		}
	}


	TNO_jamaica_investigate_interference = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_investigate
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {

		}

			factor = 50
		}

		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_investigate_interference_effect
			WIN = { clr_country_flag = TNO_WIN_investigation_happening }

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { TNO_foreign_intervention_high_us = yes }
					TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
					TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_dial_back_rhetoric = {
		icon = GFX_decision_propaganda_off

#################################
## West African Conflict (WAC) ##
#################################
USA_foreign_policy_category = {

	## CAPITULATION ##
	USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_use_force
		priority = 2000

		days_mission_timeout = 35
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no

		available = {
			CAO = { controls_state = 793 }
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = { # Success
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates_success_tt
			set_temp_variable = { tempTrust = 15 }
			USA_change_trust_in_government = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAO }
					every_enemy_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}
				CAO = { dismantle_faction = yes }

				if = { # Scenario 1
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1 }

					ZZZ = {
						TNO_WAC_clear_decision_categories = yes
						WAC_1_WAA_VICTORY = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { country_exists = YOR }
						every_country = {
							limit = { has_war_with = YOR }
							white_peace = YOR
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { # Scenario 2
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_2 }

					FFR = {
						save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
					}
					ZZZ = { country_event = { id = west_africa_peace_deal.6 hours = 1 } }
				}
				else = { # Scenario 3
					if = {
						limit = { country_exists = YOR }
						every_country = {
							limit = { has_war_with = YOR }
							white_peace = YOR
						}
					}
					ZZZ = {
						TNO_WAC_clear_decision_categories = yes
						WAC_3_FMA_VICTORY = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { # Failure
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission complete USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates_failure_tt
			USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
		}
	}

	## EQUIPMENT ##
	USA_WAC_toggle_infantry_equipment_shipments = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_visibility
		priority = 30
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			NOT = { is_ai = yes }
		}
		days_re_enable = 1

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_meeting_with_generals"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible }
				custom_effect_tooltip = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_tt_1
				clr_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_tt_2
				set_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible
			}
		}
	}
	USA_WAC_toggle_ground_vehicle_shipments = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_visibility
		priority = 20
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			NOT = { is_ai = yes }
		}
		days_re_enable = 1

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_meeting_with_generals"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = WAC_ground_vehicles_shipments_visible }
				custom_effect_tooltip = WAC_ground_vehicle_shipments_tt_1
				clr_country_flag = WAC_ground_vehicles_shipments_visible
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = WAC_ground_vehicle_shipments_tt_2
				set_country_flag = WAC_ground_vehicles_shipments_visible
			}
		}
	}

			}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_solidify_front"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_solidify_front_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = WAC_fronts_stabilized
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global.west_african_nations = THIS }
						has_war = yes
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						set_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag
						add_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = solid_frontline
						}
					}
					add_ideas = WEST_AFRICA_idea_stable_front
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_WAC_offensive_ghana = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_tank
		priority = 100

		available = {
			any_country = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAO
				OR = {
					controls_state = 827
					controls_state = 274
					controls_state = 833
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = WAC_logistics_not_saturated_tt
				NOT = { has_active_mission = USA_WAC_preparing_offensive }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = WAC_offensive_neighbor_state_tt
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = FFR
							is_in_faction_with = WOL
							is_in_faction_with = SUS
						}
						OR = {
							# States
							controls_state = 827
							controls_state = 274
							controls_state = 833

							# Neighboring States
							controls_state = 779
							controls_state = 780
							controls_state = 1208
							controls_state = 834
							controls_state = 1217
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = west_african_war_ongoing
			has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3
			OR = {
				827 = { has_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag }
				274 = { has_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag }
				833 = { has_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag }
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 827 }
			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp
		days_remove = 30
		modifier = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 }
			activate_mission = USA_WAC_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = WAC_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			WAC_escalate = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			random_state = {
				limit = { state = 827 }
				clr_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = solid_frontline
				}
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = { state = 274 }
				clr_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = solid_frontline
				}
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = { state = 833 }
				clr_state_flag = WAC_solid_frontline_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = solid_frontline
				}
			}
			activate_mission = USA_WAC_offensive_ghana_stagnate
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					state = 827
					size > 0
				}
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 827
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100

	USA_WAC_stabilize_front = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat
		priority = 101
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = WAC_fronts_stabilized }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3 }
		}

		days_remove = 7
		is_good = yes

		fire_only_once = yes

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_stabilize_front_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = WAC_fronts_stabilized
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global.west_african_nations = THIS }
						has_war = yes
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = WEST_AFRICA_idea_chaotic_front
						add_idea = WEST_AFRICA_idea_stable_front
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}
	}

	USA_coup_mali_WA = {
		icon = GFX_MAG_decision_werbell_combat_unit
		priority = 99
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3
		}
		available = {
			country_exists = MLI
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 50

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 19.99
			command_power > 19.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_20_cp_20_pp

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_coup_mali_WA"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -20 add_political_power = -20 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_coup_mali_WA_tt
			USA_decrease_optics_medium = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				KAY = {
					add_to_array = { global.WAC_contender = THIS }
					add_to_array = { global.WAC_FMA_faction = THIS }
					add_state_core = 1604
					add_state_core = 836
					add_state_core = 1227
					add_state_core = 1231
					transfer_state = 1604
					transfer_state = 836
					transfer_state = 1227
					transfer_state = 1231

					load_oob = "KAY_1962"
					TNO_startup_nation = yes

					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						add_resource = {
							type = power
							amount = 2
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { pus_temp = 1 }
					econ_pus_change = yes

					set_country_flag = FMA_MEMBER
					remove_faction_status = yes
					add_ideas = FMA_Faction
				}
				MLI = {
					remove_ideas = MLI_idea_traore_problem
					set_temp_variable = { pus_temp = -1 }
					econ_pus_change = yes
				}
				FFR = {
					add_to_faction = KAY
					every_country = {
						limit = { has_war_with = FFR }
						KAY = {
							add_to_war = {
								targeted_alliance = FFR
								enemy = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { MLI = { has_capitulated = yes } }
					KAY = {
						set_cosmetic_tag = KAY_unified
						add_state_core = 1540
						add_state_core = 1225
						add_state_core = 1230
						add_state_core = 837
						transfer_state = 1540
						transfer_state = 1225
						transfer_state = 1230
						transfer_state = 837
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			NOT = {
				CAO = { has_idea = CAO_idea_egyptian_intelligence }
			}
		}
		available = {
			is_in_faction_with = ITA
			EGY = { is_subject_of = ITA }
			OR = {
				1127 = { is_fully_controlled_by = EGY }
				1128 = { is_fully_controlled_by = EGY }
			}
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 19.99
			command_power > 4.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_5_cp_20_pp

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_italian_intelligence_WA"

			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 add_political_power = -20 }

			USA_increase_trust_in_government_medium = yes

			CAO = {

			}
		}

			USA_increase_service_manpower_depletion_rate_medium = yes

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_WAC_Increased_Draft } }

			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_WAC_divisions = 1 }

					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1 }

						days = 30
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3 }
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.209
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	### GARRISON AND DISCONTENT MISSIONS ###

	USA_WAC_garrisons_weaken = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		priority = 1000

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no

		fire_only_once = no

		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_garrisons_weaken"
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.WAC_escalation
						value = 15
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -2 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 15 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -4 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 25 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -6 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 50 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -10 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 70 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -12 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = USA_WAC_garrisons_weaken
			}
		}
	}

	USA_WAC_discontent_rises = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		priority = 1000

		days_mission_timeout = 90
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no

		fire_only_once = no

		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_discontent_rises"
			hidden_effect = { # war crimes event. Only fire once
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 75 }
					}
					country_event = { id = west_african_crisis.50 days = 14 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 50 }
					}
					country_event = { id = west_african_crisis.49 days = 14 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_wac_garrison_strength > 80 }
				}
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_small = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_wac_garrison_strength > 60 }
				}
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_medium = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_wac_garrison_strength > 40 }
				}
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
			}
			else = {
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 10 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -6 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 30 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -8 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 50 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -10 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 70 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -12 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else = {
				USA_decrease_optics_small = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_optics > 80 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_government = liberalism
							has_government = conservatism
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_all_voters_header_tt
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_pro = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_black_pro = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_pro }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_hispanic_pro = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_hispanic_pro }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_minority_pro = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_minority_pro }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_nativists_pro = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_nativists_pro }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_urban_pro = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_urban_pro }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_rural_pro = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_rural_pro }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_pro_shift

					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_nat = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_black_nat = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_black_nat }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_hispanic_nat = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_hispanic_nat }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_minority_nat = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_minority_nat }
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_nativists_nat = 1}
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_nativists_nat }

	### TROOP RESTRAINT DECISIONS ###

	USA_WAC_increase_troop_restraint = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_WAC_increase_troop_restraint_trigger_tt
				check_variable = { USA_WAC_troop_restraint < 100 }
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_WAC_increase_troop_restraint"
			set_temp_variable = { temp_value = 5 }
			USA_WAC_troop_restraint_change = yes
			USA_increase_optics_small = yes
			USA_decrease_trust_in_government_small = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_increase_troop_restraint_tt
			subtract_from_variable = { WAC_war_crimes = 1 }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	USA_WAC_decrease_troop_restraint = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_WAC_decrease_troop_restraint_trigger_tt
				check_variable = { USA_WAC_troop_restraint > 0 }
			}
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				command_power > 19.99
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_20_cp

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_WAC_decrease_troop_restraint"
			set_temp_variable = { temp_value = -5 }
			USA_WAC_troop_restraint_change = yes
			USA_decrease_optics_medium = yes
			USA_increase_trust_in_government_small = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_decrease_troop_restraint_tt
			add_to_variable = { WAC_war_crimes = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -20
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

		}

			ANG = {
				add_political_power = 100
			}

			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = OFN_Independent_Member

						has_idea = OFN_Mandate
					}
					NOT = { tag = BRA }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ANG modifier = ANG_savimbi_acknowledged }
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
	}

		days_remove = 90

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 }

			USA = { set_country_flag = US_bombing_ANG_active }

			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = ANG_bombing

				add_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { bombing_campaign }
					province = { all_provinces = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			USA = { clr_country_flag = US_bombing_ANG_active }

			FROM = {
				clr_state_flag = ANG_bombing

				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { bombing_campaign }
					province = { all_provinces = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}

USA_foreign_policy_category = { #Fetti #Marxivi
	USA_coordinate_with_australian_patrols = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_battleship
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_indonesia_selected = yes
			check_variable = { global.ICW_phase > 0 }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check_extra = t_cp_check }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { t_cp_check_extra = 0.01 }
			command_power > t_cp_check_extra
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_dynamic

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
		}

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tempDiscontent = -5 }
			INS_ICW_change_discontent = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tempEscalation = 5 }
			INS_ICW_change_escalation = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = INS }
					set_temp_variable = { v = 0.025 }
					INS_ICW_modify_recon_factor = yes
				}	
			}
			else = {
				DMP = {
					set_temp_variable = { v = 0.025 }
					INS_ICW_modify_recon_factor = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = USA_INS.200 }
			}
		}
		days_re_enable = 30
	}
	USA_prioritize_buying_indonesian_resources = {
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_indonesia_selected = yes
			check_variable = { global.ICW_phase > 0 }
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_oil_extraction
		cost = 15
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
		}
		days_re_enable = 60
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { tempDiscontent = -5 }
			INS_ICW_change_discontent = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tempEscalation = 5 }
			INS_ICW_change_escalation = yes
			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 2 }
			econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
			set_temp_variable = { temp_modifier = 15 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}

					}
				}
			}

					is_core_of = INS

					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = FRI
						is_fully_controlled_by = DMP
						is_fully_controlled_by = NII

				}
			}
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only

					province = { all_provinces = yes }
				}

					type = infrastructure
					damage = 1
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_INS_bombings = 1 }
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { targeted_bombing_campaign }
					province = { all_provinces = yes }
				}
			}
		}

							var:USA_bombing_array^i = {

							}

					}
				}

						limit = {

							}
						}
					}
				}

		}

			TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = "TNO_increase_volunteers_SAF_1"

			set_temp_variable = { proxy = SAW }
			USA_increase_service_manpower_depletion_rate_medium = yes

			SAF = { add_stability = 0.02 add_war_support = 0.02 add_political_power = 100 }
			hidden_effect = {



				if = {
					limit = { is_ai = yes }
					SAF = {
						load_oob = "SAF_American_Infantry"

						add_manpower = 5000
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment_3
							amount = 2000
							producer = USA
						}

							amount = 300
							producer = USA
						}

							}

								amount = 100

							}
						}

								type = MBT_equipment_1
								amount = 100
								producer = USA
							}
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = motorized_equipment_1

	USA_bombing_runs_gazaland = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_gazaland_selected = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 120
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 14.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 90

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_bombing_runs"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = US_aid_gazaland_simango }
				if = { #Check for whether Simango was supported and 2 countries need to be hit
					limit = { country_exists = GAZ } #Don't hit annexed countries
					GAZ = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
							days = 90
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { country_exists = GZO }
					GZO = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
							days = 90
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				GAZ = {
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
						days = 90
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_PHI_doing_preparation_decision }
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { GDP > 0 } }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_100_million

		days_remove = 20
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_PHI_comphrehensive_aid"
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { removed_from_reserves = money_reserves }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = removed_from_reserves min = 0 max = 0.10 }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = 0.10 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = removed_from_reserves }
				add_to_variable = { national_debt = to_add_to_debt }
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_PHI_doing_preparation_decision
		}
		remove_effect = {
			UPH = {
				set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = 0.25 }
				econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 250
					producer = USA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = USA
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = UPH_usa_aid_package
					days = 120
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tt_USA_PHI_GDP
			clr_country_flag = USA_PHI_doing_preparation_decision

	USA_USFIP_recon_timeout = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_philippines_war_selected = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UPH_ideology
						option = UPH_IDEOLOGY_FAILED_RECONSTRUCTION
					}
				}
				set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UPH_ideology
						option = UPH_IDEOLOGY_ROMULO
					}
				}
				set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
				set_country_flag = USA_PHI_delegitimized_leyte
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
					has_country_flag = USA_PHI_delegitimized_leyte
				}
				PHI_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_USFIP_recon_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = PHI_Blitz.22 }
				TNO_fopo_remove_philippines_reconstruction_tab = yes
			}
		}
	}
	USA_SPH_recon_timeout = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_philippines_war_selected = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPH_coalition_path
						option = SPH_COALITION_PATH_FAILED_RECONSTRUCTION
					}
				}
				set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = SPH_coalition_path
							option = SPH_COALITION_PATH_TARUC
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = SPH_coalition_path
							option = SPH_COALITION_PATH_TANADA
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
				}
				PHI_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPH_recon_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = PHI_Blitz.200 days = 30 } }
				TNO_fopo_remove_philippines_reconstruction_tab = yes
			}
		}
	}

	USA_the_african_quagmire = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat_skull
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Mandates_East_Africa_Decolonized
						has_country_flag = Mandates_Angola_Decolonized
						has_country_flag = Mandates_Central_Africa_Decolonized
					}
				}
			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = yes ###after all, you want'd to stay in and spread the good of the free world... right?

		fire_only_once = no

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { USA_mandates_cost = 0.5 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_mandates_cost max = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mandates_cost_tt
			set_temp_variable = { tempHawkishness = -1.5 }
			USA_change_hawkishness = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_mandate_protest_fired } }
				set_country_flag = USA_mandate_protest_fired
				USA_africa_shared_discontent_fire_effect = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = USA_withdraw_cost_trust } }
				set_variable = { USA_withdraw_cost_trust = -10 }
				set_variable = { USA_withdraw_pp = 300 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_withdraw_cost_available
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA_withdraw_cost_trust < -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { USA_withdraw_cost_trust = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { USA_withdraw_pp = 15 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_withdraw_cost_tt
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Mandates_Angola_collapsed }
							check_variable = { ANG.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Mandates_East_Africa_collapsed }
							check_variable = { MZB.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Mandates_Central_Africa_collapsed }
							check_variable = { COG.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
						AND = {
							has_global_flag = CAR_FORMED
							check_variable = { USC.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mandates_low_stability_warning_tt
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -5 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
				set_temp_variable = { tempTrust = -5 }
				USA_change_trust_in_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

					}
				}
			}

					limit = {
						CAL = {
							controls_state = 1237 # Puerto Plata
							controls_state = 1709 # Cibao Norte
							controls_state = 1708 # Duarte
							OR = {
								controls_state = 1710 # Cibao Sur
								controls_state = 1707 # Sureste
							}
						}
					}

					DOM = { save_global_event_target_as = losing_country }
					CAL = {
						save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
						white_peace = DOM
					}
					TNO_Puerto_Plata_closing = yes
					TNO_PPI_CAL_victory = yes

					log = "war_won"
					set_global_flag = war_won
					set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
					add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
				}
				#else_if = { # At least 50% -> Balaguer coup, ceasefire
				#	limit = {
				#		CAL = {
				#			controls_state = 1237 # Puerto Plata
				#			controls_state = 1709 # Cibao Norte
				#			controls_state = 1708 # Duarte
				#		}
				#	}
				#
				#	TNO_PPI_DOM_ceasefire = yes
				#}
				else = { # Invasion collapses
					TNO_Puerto_Plata_closing = yes
					TNO_PPI_DOM_victory = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

### Border War Stage ###
USA_foreign_policy_category = {
	USA_CLL_supply_forces = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		available = {
			var:USA.COL_faction_support = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = IBR_COL_bribing_officials
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_border_clashes_happening
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}

		cost = 50
		days_re_enable = 60

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_CLL_supply_forces"
			CLL = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = USA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 100
					producer = USA

### Civil War ! ! ###
USA_foreign_policy_category = {
	USA_CLL_send_volunteers = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_civil_war_ongoing

			OR = {
				AND = {
					CLL = {
						AND = {
							owns_state = 1662
							owns_state = 1660
							owns_state = 1659
							owns_state = 493
							owns_state = 1699
							owns_state = 1700
						}
					}
					check_variable = { USA_CLL_volunteer_counter < 3 }
				}
				AND = {
					CLL = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								owns_state = 1662
								owns_state = 1660
								owns_state = 1659
								owns_state = 493
								owns_state = 1699
								owns_state = 1700
							}
						}
					}
					check_variable = { USA_CLL_volunteer_counter < 2 }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 9.99
		}

	USA_WAFR_reconstruction_timeout = {
		icon = GFX_decision_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wafr_reconstruction_selected = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 240
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					check_variable = { WAF_average_reconstruction > 80 }
				}
				WAF_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WAF_average_reconstruction > 89 } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAFR_reconstruction_success_tt
				WAF_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAFR_reconstruction_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = free_france_reconstruction.6 }
				TNO_fopo_remove_wafr_reconstruction_tab = yes
				set_global_flag = FFR_reconstruction_failed
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = free_france_reconstruction.13 days = 32 }
			}

			clear_variable = USA_WAFR_urban_development_state
			clear_variable = USA_WAFR_naval_base_state
			clear_variable = USA_WAFR_corporate_interactions_tracker

		}
	}
